Foreign Important Telegrams

Songgang Resumes Persuading Carahan 57

Neither Side Wishes to Take the Initiative on Treaty Issues

Japan Claims to Have Established a Foundation for Future Formal Negotiations

Matsuoka Scheduled to Depart Moscow Tonight

Will Make a Brief Stop in Warsaw to Meet with Polish Authorities

National News Agency, Moscow, 5th: Following the second meeting between Matsuoka, the Japanese representative to the League of Nations, and Soviet Deputy Foreign Commissar Carahan today, reliable sources report that neither Japan nor Russia seems willing to take the initiative regarding a non-aggression treaty. Yosuke Matsuoka is striving to position Japan as being in favor of a non-aggression treaty, rather than advocating for it. Carahan, on the other hand, seeks to have Russia appear to be invited to join a non-aggression treaty, rather than proposing it himself. It is said that Matsuoka mentioned to Carahan the obstacles to concluding a non-aggression treaty soon, such as the strong opposition within Japan and the intense political infighting. He also stated that Japan is seeking to establish "Japan's true spirit" domestically, to address all issues with unity. Once this is achieved, a non-aggression treaty concerning "Manchukuo" will be easier to pursue. Carahan's attitude, it is said, has been sympathetic to a non-aggression treaty from the outset. He told Matsuoka that if a non-aggression treaty is truly beneficial to Japan, it should not be swayed by purely domestic political events. He also stated that the Soviet Union has always shown a friendly attitude towards "Manchukuo," and therefore remained neutral during General Ma Zhanshan's battles. According to unconfirmed reports, Carahan and Matsuoka will meet again tomorrow, but so far, neither side has made any concrete proposals. They are merely exchanging opinions, dispelling misunderstandings and suspicions, so that future diplomatic representatives of the puppet organization can easily make a formal proposal to both Russia and Japan to conclude such a treaty. It is also said that after discussing the possibility of a non-aggression treaty, they further discussed, in strict secrecy, the position Japan will take in Geneva, with the conversation lasting about an hour. Matsuoka will now postpone his departure from Moscow until Monday evening to attend the 15th anniversary of the Soviet Revolution. According to Matsuoka's staff, he will make a brief stop in Warsaw en route to visit Polish dignitaries, but will not discuss diplomatic issues. He also plans to stay in Paris for two or three days before going to Geneva.

National News Agency, Moscow, 5th: It is claimed tonight that Carahan and Yosuke Matsuoka will again discuss issues related to the puppet organization, as both sides feel that although these issues have not yet reached a concrete conclusion, mutual understanding has increased significantly.

Dentsu News Agency, Moscow, 5th: After the second meeting between Matsuoka and Carahan today, Matsuoka's representative told reporters that the meeting with Carahan aimed to guide Japanese-Russian relations towards general goodwill. This free conversation has now concluded, and although it was purely a personal meeting, it can be considered a gain on the way to Geneva.

Dentsu, Moscow, 5th: Matsuoka's representative's staff, including Secretary Kiichi Nakashio and nine others, departed from the Russian capital at 10:00 PM on the 5th as the advance team, heading directly to Paris to deliver a draft of Matsuoka's representative's opinion to Representative Nagaoka and other representatives stationed in Europe.

Police Department Uncovers Reactionary Organization 58

The Tenko-kai and the Seinen-sha Have Close Ties

Plotting to Launch a Riot During the Grand Military Exercise to Overthrow the Government

Leader of the Seinen-sha on the Run, Treasonous Documents Discovered

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 6th: The Metropolitan Police Department, with lightning speed, carried out a major crackdown on right-wing groups. The lead came from the confession of the head of the Murasakiyama Juku, who was arrested in connection with the May 15th Incident. During interrogation, he stated, "All confessions must wait until after the 10th. After the 10th, things can be revealed." His tone suggested that there were major conspiracies surrounding him. Around the 20th of last month, an explosion, like fireworks, occurred on the upper floor of the Independent Seinen-sha, a right-wing organization. Internal investigation revealed that the Seinen-sha had close ties with the Tenko-kai, led by Hidesan Toyama, the Murasakiyama Juku head's mentor.

Further internal investigation revealed that the Independent Seinen-sha and the Tenko-kai were planning to assassinate high-ranking officials during the Grand Military Exercise while they were in the provinces, simultaneously attacking power plants, to overthrow the government in one fell swoop. The Independent Seinen-sha was founded by Yoshio Kodama (30 years old) after leaving the Kenkoku-kai. During the search of the organization's headquarters yesterday, bombs, pistols, Japanese swords, and a treasonous document signed by Toshio Okada (who has already been arrested) were discovered. The document strongly advocated for the expulsion of established political parties, financial cliques, and "treacherous ministers," implying direct action. Furthermore, their core members seemed to have participated in the May 15th attack on power plants. Hidesan Toyama, the leader of the Tenko-kai, also has important connections with blood oath assassination groups. The reason why such figures as Nissei Inoue were able to avoid the Metropolitan Police Department's intensive search and arrest was because they were hiding in the Tenko-kai headquarters. Kodama, the leader of the Seinen-sha, has now fled and is missing. A rigorous search is currently underway.

Nihon Rengo News Agency, Tokyo, 6th: The reasons for the Metropolitan Police Department's crackdown on Hidesan Toyama, the third son of right-wing leader Mitsuru Toyama, are as follows: (1) He supplied six pistols to the influential figure Zizan Juku, head of Murasakiyama in the May 15th case. (2) He extorted 200 yen in cash from Kichigoro Akanuma and Sadami Yamamoto, the perpetrators of the Tokyo Gas Company incident, who were arrested in September. (3) He played an important role in a plot to assassinate a certain high-ranking official. The Metropolitan Police Department is scheduled to escort Toyama to the Ichigaya Prison on the 7th. Nakagawa, Yamamoto, Yoshioka, and others who were arrested at the same time as Toyama are not directly related to the May 15th Incident, but are perpetrators of the gas extortion incident.

French Radical Party's Far East Foreign Policy 59

Advocates for the Use of International Conventions

to Resolve the Sino-Japanese Dispute

Will Not Protect Aggressor Nations

Due to Commercial Interests

International Telegraph Agency, Paris, 6th: The French Radical Party held its national party congress in Toulouse. During the meeting, Representative Cote gave a speech mentioning French foreign policy, stating that since the party (referring to the Radical Party) now holds the reins of power in France, it must advocate for the resolution of the Sino-Japanese issue according to the plan suggested by the League of Nations report. France's policy should never protect aggressor nations due to commercial interests, but should support the invaded nation. Herriot also stated in this regard that France's stance on the Sino-Japanese issue is to advocate for its resolution in accordance with justice and various conventions. This expression by the French, as well as the declaration made by the French representative Bérenger in Geneva yesterday, stating that the French advocate for the resolution of the Sino-Japanese issue using the Nine-Power Treaty, etc., and do not recognize the validity of any nation obtaining territory of another nation by force, all demonstrate the attitude of the French representatives at future League of Nations meetings regarding the Sino-Japanese issue.

Franco-German Rapprochement Is an Urgent Priority 60

Havas News Agency, Toulouse, 5th: The Radical Party congress discussed foreign policy this afternoon, with a very crowded attendance. The chairman declared to the entire audience that Spanish Representative Garces was present, and the entire audience stood and applauded their welcome. Then Representative Detton, who was sent to the League of Nations as the French representative, rose to speak, saying that in order for the international situation to move towards détente, Franco-German rapprochement is essential. He also said that the current urgent task is not to compete in increasing armaments, but to achieve universal disarmament. To achieve this goal, the only way is to implement the arms reduction plan proposed by the French government. Garces said, "The ideal declared by the French Revolution is universal brotherhood. Even with the troubles of neighboring countries, it can still uphold this principle. This is what people know today." Representative Cote then rose to speak, saying that universal disarmament is a condition for the security of all nations, and that the French plan will surely enable the disarmament conference to be successful. The congress then passed a motion stating, in essence, that the Radical Party requests the government to implement its foreign policy in accordance with the spirit of the League of Nations, strive for the cooperation of all nations, and expresses its confidence in the government to work towards the success of disarmament, so as to ease the feelings of all nations and guarantee equality in the security of all nations.

Russo-French Non-Aggression Pact Under Negotiation 61

Havas, Toulouse, 5th: Prime Minister Herriot revisited the Radical Party Congress and issued a declaration, the last part of which is briefly recorded as follows: Prime Minister Herriot confirmed the matter of France and the Soviet Union negotiating a mutual non-aggression treaty, but said, "The existing agreements will not be changed as a result. There is no doubt that the reason Britain participated in the European War was because it had signed a treaty guaranteeing Belgium's neutrality. If all the signatures on all treaties have the same value as Britain's signature, then peace can be regarded as fully guaranteed." Herriot also deeply admired Foreign Minister Bérenger's support for Briand's advocacy of peace. Regarding the issue of equality in armaments, Herriot said that if such a method contains the intention of restoring armaments, it cannot be recognized under any circumstances. If its intention is to consolidate public security, then France is prepared to accept it. Finally, Herriot also analyzed and explained the arms plan proposed by France.

Havas, Rome, 6th: Norman Davis, the head of the US delegation to the Disarmament Conference, will soon come to Rome to meet with Prime Minister Mussolini, as well as the Italian Ambassador to the United States and representative to the League of Nations, Commissioner Rosso for the Disarmament Conference. Davis' trip to Rome, after his travels to London and Paris, is of particular value. Why are Russian Ships in the Bay of Danzig? 63

National News Agency, Warsaw, 5th: Several ships of the Soviet Russian Baltic Fleet suddenly appeared near the Polish naval port of Gdynia in the Bay of Danzig, and it is said that Soviet Russian Minister of Military Affairs Voroshilov was also on the Marat flagship. As a result, Polish public opinion has become greatly alarmed and demands that the government urgently lodge a serious protest with the Soviet Russian authorities, considering this an infringement of Polish sovereignty, as the arrival of the Soviet Russian fleet was not notified to the Polish authorities in advance.

German Parliamentary Re-elections Held Yesterday 64

National News Agency, Berlin, 6th: This morning, 44 million German voters will go to the provinces, where 35 million people will vote to elect members of the eighth post-war parliament. Many people expect this to be the last parliament elected according to the current constitution and electoral system, as both the National Socialist Party and the Communist Party are, in principle, opposed to the parliamentary system. The government party hopes that the constitutional reforms planned by Papen and his colleagues will fundamentally transform the next parliament. Currently, only the middle-class parties, the Bavarian People's Party, the Catholic Center Party, and the Social Democratic Party are willing to continue with the current constitution with slight modifications. Therefore, today's vote is essentially an expression of support for and opposition to parliament. Voting began at 9:00 AM and ended at 6:00 PM. The first to vote were President Hindenburg and then Prime Minister Papen, both at Wilhelmstrasse. The people greeted them with cheers. The streets were very quiet, as all demonstrations had been banned since midnight.

Havas, Berlin, 6th: On the eve of the election, it rained appropriately, and there were almost no pedestrians on the streets. Berlin was shrouded in an atmosphere of mystery and unease, similar to the situation in Germany. The leaders of the various parties planned to issue final speeches in the evening, appealing to the people. Among them, one speech was particularly interesting, that of Center Party leader Kaas. Kaas did not attack the National Socialist Party at all, but expressed serious opposition to the current political system in serious terms, believing that the current optimism of Prime Minister Papen was similar to the optimism of the German government at the end of the Great War in 1918. He also criticized the government's foreign policy, saying, "The government protests against the various treaties imposed on Germany by other countries, but in domestic affairs, the government uses the same methods that foreign countries use to deal with the German people." Kaas also issued a serious warning in his conclusion, saying, "We will not become a revolutionary party, but legal resistance is more difficult to overcome than the obstacles set up by traitors."

Reuters, Berlin, 6th: It is estimated that by 2:30 PM today, about 40% of voters had voted. Everything was peaceful. Two police aircraft flew in the sky, so that if unrest was spotted, it could be reported to headquarters by radio. Today, several buses were seen on the road, heavily guarded by police. The subway was running further and further away.

Havas, Berlin, 6th: Berlin is very quiet. The transport strike has eased slightly. Some trams are running on the streets, and several subway lines are open, but buses are still absent. As of noon, no serious incidents have occurred throughout Germany.

US Election Campaign to Conclude Soon 70

Hoover Market Has Become a Thing of the Past, Master of the White House Will Belong to Roosevelt

North American Special Dispatch: The United States, with its eternal prosperity, is indeed extremely extravagant when prosperous, reaching its peak. But the more people enjoy themselves, the more ordinary their general life becomes. The films exported from the United States to the East and even around the world are sufficient to represent this aspect of ordinary life. However, since 1929, especially this year, the number of hungry people has increased, and the miserable state of veterans gathering in Washington makes people feel an overwhelming sense of nostalgia. ("The so-called motherland of many beggars, most people show signs of malnutrition") In the United States, there should be no such dangerous situation, right? But the reality is not so. Especially in the past year, it has become very poor. There are particularly many unemployed people. Cities are full of people looking for work. In the countryside, things cannot be sold, and even if they can be sold, they cannot be sold at a good price. If we look at it from our old habits, this is really a strange thing. Mountains of flour are piled up there, but people will starve to death. Warehouses of cloth are piled up there, but many people have no clothes to wear. The steel industry, the automobile industry, etc., have also suffered a setback. There is a lot of equipment, but there is no way to start work. The cash in the Federal Reserve has flowed out slightly this year, but it is still no less than 40 million US dollars, but the general public is still very poor. The capitalist American countryside is almost returning to the primitive agricultural era.

The "Hoover Market" was once extremely prosperous. The whole country sang and worshiped him. The president of the United States, although not as majestic as the emperor of the East, can rule peacefully for four years after he is elected, and realize his political ambitions without hindrance. When Mr. Hoover first came to power, he was indeed admired by women, and he implicitly guided the world with (national) power. However, after the economic panic struck, it was similar to Germany. Vast financial capital had no resistance. The talented and meticulous President Hoover had to burn the midnight oil and tried various methods of relief, but in the end, they were ineffective. In the blink of an eye, the four-year term is about to expire. The period of wind and rain has not yet passed, and the election period has come again. To incite the same market as in 1929, it is probably impossible in fact. However, we must try our best. Therefore, since the presidential candidate was designated, various stocks have risen sharply by more than double. But after all, the effect of air is vain, and it has fallen again after September. Although the Democratic Party does not have as many major industrial capitalists as the Republican Party, it has indeed gained the trend of winning the majority of voters in recent years. Although most of the presidents in American history belong to the Republican Party, the recent Democratic Party has risen twice. Let's look at the recent five presidents. Wilson County served twice (1913-1921). It was a Democratic regime. In addition, Harding, Coolidge, and Hoover were all Republican victories. As far as we induce, all re-elected presidents can be elected. What's more, Roosevelt, who is competing with Mr. Hoover this time, has a personal physique, which is not very healthy (he has suffered from paralysis). He is not fully healed yet. To stand up and compete with Hoover, there are inevitably many difficulties in fact. This is the trend in the early stages of the campaign.

As for the political platforms of the two parties, I think the newspapers in the country must have already recorded them, so there is no need to repeat them. Moreover, their political platforms are very ordinary, and there is nothing special about them. However, only two points are worth mentioning. The first is that since the promulgation of the Prohibition Law, most Americans have been drooling and hoping to lift the ban immediately. Therefore, although the Republican Party advocates Prohibition, it also indicates that it tends to amend the Prohibition Law. The Democratic Party directly advocates opening liquor tickets. The second is the issue of restoring the market and relieving unemployment. The Republican Party still adheres to the policy of protecting trade and defends its past efforts to restore the declining market. It also says that it has now been completed and the market has begun to retreat. On the Democratic Party side, it opposes protecting tariffs and opposes unreasonable overseas investment of hard-earned money. At the same time, it also advocates providing jobs for the unemployed. The two figures standing at the forefront of the election campaign are giving speeches everywhere, broadcasting on the radio, etc., turning over and over, all saying this kind of thing. Whether the current bad market has already begun to retreat, and whether financial tariffs can alleviate the current economic panic, we know if we use a calm mind and think carefully, it is still a problem.

However, the issue that occupies the most space in major American newspapers and is the most talked about event in the streets is still the election issue. Who is the winner of the election, Hoover or Roosevelt? Several major chambers in this city (New York) have conducted trial voting, and Roosevelt always wins more. At the same time, since 1921, the Republican Party has elected three presidents in a row, and the public is inevitably somewhat tired of Mr. Hoover. Regarding Prohibition, relieving unemployment, and restoring the market, they all feel that the Republican Party is not very competent. Therefore, the "Hoover Market" has become a thing of the past, and the future master of the White House is probably going to change people. What will the result be? It will be able to fully know on October 12th (October 12, 1932 in New York)

The Situation in Sichuan Becomes Increasingly Chaotic 71

Liu Xiang Launches General Offensive on Luzhou, Sets Deadline for Capture

Deng, Tian, and Liu Collude to Open Chongqing and Wanxian

Zhang Qun Discusses Sichuan Affairs in Detail with Various Representatives

Hankou Correspondence: Since Liu Wenhui and Deng Xihou, Tian Songyao reached an understanding, and there were rumors of a Chengdu conference, the situation in Sichuan has suddenly changed and is becoming increasingly chaotic. The strengths of the two Lius are essentially equal. The Chongqing side has a total of six divisions and various commanders' troops, totaling over 100 regiments, with more than 110,000 men. The provincial side also has six divisions and various troops, totaling about 90 regiments, with more than 104,000 men. Without the participation of a third party, it is impossible to determine victory or defeat. The forces of Deng and Tian thus hold significant weight. The two Lius are both doing their utmost to win them over as allies. Unexpectedly, Deng and Tian, while feigning compliance with Liu Xiang, continued to negotiate with Liu Wenhui, eventually reaching an agreement due to their long-standing close relationship as alumni, aiming to restrain Liu Xiang. Recently, the generals of the three divisions of Liu, Deng, and Tian, including Sun Decao, Dong Chang'an, Chen Shunong, Xiang Youren, Leng Yindong, Liu Fanjiu, etc., have met several times in Chengdu to discuss solutions thoroughly. Liu Xiang's side is desperately denying that Deng and Tian have taken this action, and Deng and Tian's side has not yet made any explicit statements. However, even the slightest clues are enough to warrant careful study. The sudden change in Deng and Tian's attitude may lead some to suspect that they will join forces with Liu Wenhui to attack Liu Xiang, but that is not the case. Deng and Tian benefit from the coexistence of the two Lius, as they check each other. Therefore, when the provincial Liu was strong, they allied with Liu Xiang; after the Chongqing Liu won, they compromised with Liu Wenhui. If Liu Xiang fails in his attack on Luzhou, Deng and Tian will inevitably be the ones to maintain Liu Xiang's position. However, aside from securing a portion of Liu Wenhui's defense area, the two Deng and Tian have other ambitions. What is their purpose? It is to open Chongqing and Wanxian. If Deng and Tian's goal is this, why wouldn't Yang Sen, Liu Cunhou, etc. also think the same? Moreover, the circular telegram sent by the second-tier generals originated from Chongqing, and the leading signatory was Tang Shizun, the division commander of the Chongqing army. The essence of the telegram is to break down defense zones. In the future, when Deng, Tian, Yang, and Liu raise the slogan of opening Chongqing and Wanxian, it will be difficult for Liu Xiang to refute them. However, he may not accept it so readily, so the extent of the chaos in Sichuan is something that we cannot predict today. Liu Xiang has long considered this point, so before Deng and Tian explicitly reveal their attitude, he is doing his utmost to maintain a false alliance, hoping to capture Luzhou and Neijiang in one fell swoop as a preemptive measure. On the 4th, he issued a second general offensive order, with three routes advancing on Luzhou. The vanguard is only 60 li away from Luzhou. The troops attacking Neijiang have also reached the border. Aircraft and warships are all at the front, and he is encouraging the soldiers to capture Luzhou and Neijiang within the deadline. A major battle is about to begin in the coming days. The Sichuan warlords are good at infighting, perhaps due to their inherent nature. As for the prolongation of the war and the suffering of the people, they hardly care. The central government and Chiang Kai-shek are now trying to get the two Lius to cease fighting. Chiang has strictly prohibited the transportation of munitions to Sichuan. Central Committee members Dai Chuanxian and Zhang Qun's arrival in Hankou also bears a significant mission in this regard. On the 5th, Liu Xiang's representative Qiu Jia, Deng Xihou's representative Cao Chichang, and Tian Songyao's representative Yang Jintang, etc., paid a visit to Zhang, presenting their opinions in detail and urging Zhang to visit Sichuan. It is said that Zhang indicated that as long as it is beneficial to Sichuan, going there is not out of the question, but now is not the time. Some representatives expressed concern that the governing edict for Sichuan issued by the National Government in its 17th year, and the ten measures proposed by the Central Committee members in Shanghai, may not be familiar with the situation in Sichuan and may still not be easy to implement in the future. They requested Zhang to draft another plan and submit it to Chiang for review. (November 5th)

The Atrocities of the Japanese Army in Fushun 72

Over Two Thousand Residents of Pingdingshan Massacred

Beiping Correspondence: A gentleman who arrived in Beiping from Fushun yesterday spoke in detail about the situation in the county under the Japanese army's ravages. More than two thousand residents of Pingdingshan were massacred by Japanese machine guns, which can be described as extremely tragic. The details are as follows:

Fushun County is located directly east of Liaoning Province, more than 70 li from the provincial capital. The Japanese operate coal mines and oil factories in Qianjinzhai, which belongs to the county. Since the September 18th Incident last year, before the establishment of the puppet state, the county government was reorganized almost five or six times in one month, all under the direction of Japanese advisors. The personnel of the county government and other agencies were merely used as servants. After the puppet organization was established, the heads of various agencies in the county, such as public security, finance, and education bureaus, were all replaced by Japanese-appointed pro-Japanese traitors. Those who were insincere or whose actions were slightly suspicious were put to death once discovered, so everyone was in danger and unsure of their fate. As a result, on September 4th, the Public Security Brigade revolted. The brigade commander, Li, and the deputy brigade commander, Xing, fearing Japanese suspicion and potential misfortune, secretly discussed the revolt and united the villagers in response. At one time, no less than several hundred people rose up in rebellion. In the beginning, they did not come into contact with the Japanese army, only leading their troops to station in the area bordering Xinfu in the south of the county. Thirteen Japanese soldiers went to Dadongzhou Village in the sixth district of the south of the county on September 8th for patrol and had lunch at the village chief's house. The villagers then attacked, killing one Japanese soldier and wounding another. The rest fled to Qianjinzhai Street. At 4 PM that afternoon, the Japanese army and the puppet army rushed to the village in large trucks to provide reinforcements. They killed anyone they saw upon entering the village. Fortunately, the villagers had fled in advance, so they burned seven houses in the village. Unexpectedly, at 8 AM the next morning, the Japanese army returned with hundreds of puppet soldiers and police, attacking Dadongzhou Village again, being extremely vicious, and leaving no chickens or dogs alive. They killed more than 20 villagers and set fire to all the houses in the village, destroying more than 500 rooms. All belongings were lost. Innocent villagers were brutally murdered, which is unprecedented. This is a rough account of the disaster in Dadongzhou Village in the county.

After the incident in early September, the Japanese army would occasionally patrol the villages. In any village that was suspected of being involved with the Big Swords or Volunteer Army, they would burn the village. A total of seven villages, large and small, were burned. Later, the Japanese transferred a thousand puppet guerrillas from Shenyang, led by Japanese officers to pursue the Volunteer Army. Although the Volunteer Army had a strength of four thousand, they dared not fight back due to the lack of guns and ammunition. When the Japanese army arrived at a village that the Volunteer Army had passed through, they would burn the village. The puppet guerrillas protested this inhuman act, saying that if such atrocities were to continue, they would lead their troops back to the province. The Japanese army then slightly stopped the burning of villages everywhere. On the night of September 15th (the Mid-Autumn Festival), about 800 Big Swordsmen suddenly came to Qianjinzhai Street, attacking from Pingdingshan Village in the east of the village. The Japanese army led the puppet police to fight, but they were unable to break through due to insufficient strength. The next day, the Japanese army suspected that the residents of Pingdingshan were colluding with the Big Swords Society, so they drove all the villagers, men, women, old and young, into a large pit in the southwest of the village, totaling more than 2,500 people, surrounded them on three sides, and opened fire with machine guns. All the villagers were brutally killed. Those who were not dead were searched for by the Japanese army with bayonets. Those who were found alive under the bodies were stabbed to death with bayonets. None of the more than 2,500 people survived. Their cruelty and brutality are unprecedented in the world. This is a general account of the villagers of Pingdingshan being killed.

The number of villagers in other villages who were innocently killed by the Japanese army is even more uncountable. The dates, names of the villages burned, and the number of deaths and injuries are listed below:

Village Name Date Number of Deaths

Dadongzhou September 9th 16

Xiaodongzhou September 9th 5

Qianjinzhai September 16th 3

Pingdingshan September 16th 2,500

Lizigou September 18th 2

Sijiazi September 24th 1

Xiawazi September 20th 3

Xiong Bin Arrives in Jinan, Will Go to Yexian 73

Jinan Correspondence: After the Ministry of Military Affairs issued an order to resolve the Jiaodong dispute, it also appointed Jiang Bocheng, Gao Lingbai, and Xiong Bin to supervise the withdrawal and transfer of troops from both sides. Jiang Bocheng remained in Jinan to supervise the Third Route Army, while Gao Lingbai, after contacting Shen Honglie, just arrived in Jinan from Qingdao and is scheduled to return to Qingdao at 10 PM tonight to board the Zhenhai warship with the marines to take over defenses in Yantai on the 5th. Xiong Bin, Director of the General Affairs Department of the General Staff Headquarters, departed from Beijing on the evening of the 3rd and arrived in Jinan on the Pingpu 202 train at 6 PM tonight. Han Fuju and Jiang Bocheng, etc., all went to the station to welcome him. When the press went to visit him, Xiong said that he came here on orders to go to Yexian to supervise the 21st Division. Chairman Han has obeyed the central government's orders, and Liu Zhennian has also repeatedly telegraphed the ministry to express his obedience. The Jiaodong incident can thus be peacefully resolved. However, although the Third Route Army has withdrawn, the administrative officials appointed by the provincial government are still in the defense area. The maintenance of local security and the safety of the administrative personnel of the provincial government within the defense area are extremely important. As for the withdrawal plan, the first step is for the navy to go to Yantai, and after the Third Route Army takes over the defense duties, it will go to the vicinity of Yexian. Before I departed from Beijing yesterday, I sent a telegram to Liu Zhennian, informing him of my scheduled departure. Because the telegram was forwarded by Yantai, it was very slow, so I have not yet received a reply. (November 4th)

Northern Fujian Red Bandits Retreat to the Jiangxi Border 74

Liu's Division Enters Jianyang and Jiangle

Fuzhou Correspondence: After the Red bandits Zhu De and Lin Biao's forces rampaged through northern Fujian from eastern Jiangxi, Mao Bingwen and Chen Cheng's armies from Jiangxi had advanced to Lichuan and Guangchang. Fearing that their route of return would be cut off, Zhu first withdrew from Jianning to Shicheng on the Jiangxi border to maintain rear communications, leaving only Lin Biao's force in Tai'ning to command the bandits in Shaowu and Guangze. However, the original plan for the Red bandits' entry into Fujian was to advance simultaneously on the northwest routes, but now that the west route has been withdrawn, the north route is also shaken and dares not go deep. Therefore, starting the day before yesterday, they first transported all the looted salt, rice, cloth, and cotton to their old nest on the Fujian-Jiangxi border (in the mountains bordering Tai'ning and Guangchang) for winter supplies. Then, the troops retreated along the original route. Liu Hemei, commander of the 56th Division, telegraphed the province from Jian'ou yesterday to report that there were no traces of bandits in Jianyang and Jiangle counties. The bandits in Shaowu and Guangze counties are also heading towards Tai'ning. He has now ordered the Liu Shangzhi Brigade stationed in Jian'ou to enter Jianyang, and the Gui Zhenyuan Brigade stationed in Shunchang to enter Jiangle and advance towards Shaowu and Guangze. However, after this great calamity, the local population is displaced, and their savings are exhausted. There is an urgent need to gather the refugees and return them to their homes and allocate funds for relief. The authorities are currently coordinating measures. In addition, the defense forces of the provincial capital have recently been transferred to Putian, Xianyou, Minqing, Gutian, and Yongtai counties to deploy defenses, and the military strength is quite weak. The provincial government has transferred the second regiment of the first marine brigade of the stationed Xiamen garrison, commanded by Huang Maohe, and the 183rd brigade of the 61st Division stationed in Quanzhou, commanded by Zhang Yan, to the province for garrison duty. Huang's regiment arrived in the province yesterday and is stationed in the Jiangnan area. Zhang's brigade will also arrive tomorrow and is scheduled to be stationed inside the city and outside the east, west, and north gates.

The Aviation Corps organized by the Pacification Headquarters has also been established, appointing Yang Anyu as the brigade commander, and Deng Yueming and Liu Zhiyan as deputy brigade commanders, with an office set up at the Wangzhuang Airport outside the Shuibu Gate. It has seven aircraft under its jurisdiction, namely one in Fuzhou, four in Xiamen, and two in Zhangzhou. As for the aircraft purchased with donations from overseas Chinese, five can be obtained from the French territory, ten from the British territory, and ten from the American territory, which are also being negotiated. (November 3rd)

Guangdong Province Reorganizes Local Defense Forces 75

First, Inspectors are Sent to Investigate Various Regions

The Province Plans to Establish Defense Offices by Region

Guangzhou Correspondence: The military authorities of Guangdong Province have recently planned to reorganize the local defense forces throughout the province in order to establish a foundation for local self-defense military strength. According to the plan, after the current five Pacification District Offices are abolished, a Provincial Defense Headquarters will be organized to facilitate command and control. The organizational methods of the Defense Headquarters have been handed over to the Military Affairs Office of the First Army Group Headquarters for drafting. Recently, a draft of over 50 articles has been completed. The headquarters has now submitted it to the General Staff Office for review. The outline is to divide the provincial defense forces into five districts for jurisdiction. However, the establishment of the defense districts involves the issue of the existence and abolition of the Pacification District Offices, which the authorities must carefully consider. It is currently the winter defense season, and the defense forces in various regions are working to suppress bandits and stabilize the local area. If there are any reforms to the pacification system, it will affect the current pacification efforts in various districts. Therefore, the headquarters has been holding meetings with senior military officers for several days to discuss the emergence of the Defense Headquarters and the existence and abolition of the five Pacification District Offices in detail. On the 29th of last month, the First Army Group Headquarters held another meeting, attended by the chiefs of the headquarters and the members of the Pacification District Offices, totaling over 20 people. As a result, it was decided that the current Pacification District Offices would be temporarily maintained and continue to implement the original pacification plan, but the county defense forces would be directly managed by each district. Each district will set up a Defense Office to command the defense forces in the district and actively engage in reorganization. Only after the training of the local defense forces in each county is completed will the Pacification District Offices be abolished. The headquarters has sent out several defense inspectors to various districts to inspect the east, south, west, and central regions to plan the reorganization of the defense forces. The inspector of the east region set out today (the 1st), and the rest will follow suit. Once the inspectors return to the province after their investigation, the plan to reorganize the defense forces throughout the province will be implemented. The reorganization plan for the defense forces drafted by the Military Affairs Office roughly imitates the organization of the militia in Guangxi Province. The province will be divided into several defense districts, with one commander of the general defense force in each district, and one commander in each county, who will be concurrently held by the county magistrate. The original defense force commander will then be reassigned as the deputy commander. However, this plan can only be realized after the training of the defense forces in each county has reached a considerable level. (November 1st)

The Current Situation in Qinghai 76

Gaolan Correspondence: Qinghai is located on the western frontier, and coupled with inconvenient transportation, little is known about the internal situation of Qinghai. I have long had the determination to travel there, but due to various reasons, I did not go until the time of the Qinghai Sea Sacrifice this year. The round trip took twenty-seven days. Traveling in this short period of time, coupled with unfamiliarity with the place and language barriers with the Mongolians and Tibetans, it is naturally impossible to conduct a detailed investigation. I can only write down a few words about what I saw and heard to report to the readers.

(1) The Sea Sacrifice The origin of the Sea Sacrifice is often shrouded in superstition, but after experiencing it, I will describe it for what it is worth. In the second year of the Yongzheng reign of the Qing Dynasty, Wang's army was dispatched to conquer the rebel party of Arbutan Wenbu. When they pursued them to the Ikharj River on the north bank of Nuoer (i.e., Qinghai), the men and horses were very thirsty and could not find water. Suddenly, a spring gushed out, trickling into a stream. The soldiers and horses drank and were no longer tired. The crowd cheered and bravely captured the rebel leader. The governor-general reported to the Qing court that Qinghai had been efficacious, and the Qing court ordered the god of Qinghai to be enshrined, and a monument was erected to pay tribute. This is the origin of the annual Sea Sacrifice.

Page 7

Important News Updates 77

Also, according to the regulations of the former Court of Colonial Affairs, a sea sacrifice in Qinghai was mandatory every year, and all the princes and dukes from various places were required to gather and participate. Absence without a valid reason would result in a report by high-ranking officials and a three-year salary deduction for the Jasak. It was also stipulated that the Qinghai Minister would annually convene the Jasaks for an alliance meeting. Later, due to the inconvenience of traveling back and forth, the sea sacrifice and alliance meeting were combined into one event, which has continued unchanged to this day.

The journey starts from Xining, goes out of the west gate, crosses Tongji Bridge, and travels 25 miles west along the south bank of the Huangshui River, passing Yinshantang, and then another 25 miles to Zhenhaibao. Traditionally, the sea sacrifice is held every year, and the Xining County prepares meals here, and the chief official in charge of the sea sacrifice has a snack here. Because the reporter was traveling with Zhong Xingzai, the representative of the Xi'an Pacification Headquarters, he had the pleasure of enjoying a hearty meal of mutton. After ten miles, cross the Huangshui Bridge to Zhamalong, and travel along the north bank of the Huangshui River, entering the Xishi Gorge. After 30 miles, you reach Huangyuan City. Huangyuan, formerly known as Dangar, is an important town in Qinghai. Tibetan people and people of various counties of the Republic, Guide, and Dulan come to trade here every year after September, bringing all kinds of furs, antlers, musk, and other goods to exchange for grain and tea. Merchants from the mainland who are familiar with the Tibetan language can all make profits here. Therefore, commerce is more prosperous here than in other counties. However, in August of the 18th year of the Republic, the Hui bandits captured the city, killing 3,000 people, and many shops and houses were burned. Therefore, the vitality has not yet recovered, and the market is bleak. The climate here is very cold, and the residents have a strong addiction to alcohol. Every family's wine jars are never empty. When drinking, they exchange toasts and insist on getting drunk. They don't stop until they take off their hats, expose their heads, and collapse on the ground. After getting drunk, they stumble on the road, and even close relatives do not care about them. There are five schools in the city, including one senior primary school, three junior primary schools, and one two-level girls' school. Traveling south from here for 60 miles, you reach Tu'ergan, next to Dongquo Temple, which is the main temple of the inner eight Hutuktu Kuo Buddhas. After 30 miles, you reach Riyue Mountain, which is the border between Huangyuan and the Republic counties. There is a boundary stone on the south side of the mountain, inscribed with "Southwest Boundary of Fangal." Although the mountain peak is small, the climate is cold because the terrain is even higher than Xining. The only food is green barley, and barley and oats can still mature. There are houses on the north side of the mountain, hidden in the hills and valleys, which are said to be people from the mainland who fled here due to famine. To the south, the grass is lush, and the view is desolate, with no villages. After 30 miles, you reach Chahan City, the site of the sea sacrifice, which belongs to the northwest of the Republic County, 120 miles northeast of Huangyuan. The city was built by Na Yan, the Governor-General of Shaanxi and Gansu in the third year of Daoguang in the Qing Dynasty, to station troops, set up defenses, and control the wild tribes. In the sixth year of Xianfeng, the defense was withdrawn, and the city was also abandoned. Now there is only a circle of earthen walls, and the battlements have collapsed. There are several public offices inside, most of which have collapsed. Outside the city to the north is the Sea God Temple, where the Qinghai Chief Officer comes every autumn to sacrifice to the sea. To the west is General's Terrace. This area is purely populated by the Qianbulu tribe of Tibetan people, who all live in tents, mostly near the water's edge. From a distance, they look like ashes left after cooking, and it is difficult for those unfamiliar with them to distinguish them. Looking west, the Qinghai Lake is azure blue, like a large piece of brocade being washed. Unfortunately, due to time constraints, I could not go to the shore for a closer look.

Qinghai Lake has a circumference of more than 500 miles and an area of 18,500 square miles. The water surface is 10,500 feet above sea level. The deepest part of the water is about 120 feet. The water is very clear and tastes salty and delicious. There are many fish in the water, but the Tibetan people are not used to eating fish. Therefore, there are many fish in the lake. In recent years, some people have been catching and selling them to the mainland. The yellow fish from Lanzhou are caught from Qinghai Lake. In summer, fishermen dig canals along the coast and divert water to the grassland. The fish then gather along the canals in dense grass. Fishermen kill them with sticks, open their bellies, remove their internal organs, and lay them on the ground. The ground is rich in salt, so they do not rot. After drying, they are transported to the mainland for sale. In winter, the seawater freezes, and fishermen chisel ice to get fish, called frozen fish, which are also transported and sold to the mainland. There are two islands in the sea, one is called Haixin Mountain, and the other is called Haixin West Mountain. There are small temples on them, and Tibetan monks who practice Zen meditation here come out in winter when the ice is solid to get a year's worth of food to live in. It is said that the water force is very weak, and even a mustard seed cannot float. In the summer of 1907, Mr. Kochzlov, a member of the Russian Royal Geographical Society, reached Haixin Mountain with a sailboat, causing great fear among the Mongolians, who thought it was a god. When Nian Gengyao conquered Qinghai, the residents said it was the god of the sea, because the sea water surged when Nian arrived, so it was the sea dragon coming to court. There is a salt pond in the southwest of the sea, which produces a very large amount of salt, with a blue color and delicious taste. It is easy to collect. Just break the salt crust of the small pond with a hammer, and you can take it at will. Without manufacturing, it is a fine product. After taking it, the water will form a crust again after a month, and salt will grow inside again. It can be taken in a cycle endlessly, and it is transported by Tibetan people with yaks, and others cannot. Because the road is far and sparsely populated, bandits often rob and kill pedestrians. The Sea God Temple is 50 miles from the sea and was built by Qing Shu, the Xining Affairs Minister in the 33rd year of Guangxu in the Qing Dynasty. The buildings are extremely simple and crude. There are several wing rooms inside, which are badly damaged. To the north is the Sea God Hall. In the center of the hall is a stone tablet with the inscription "The God of Qinghai Manifests." Every autumn, the Qinghai authorities send letters to summon the Mongolian princes and dukes for the annual alliance ceremony, which is held at this temple.

In the past, the sea sacrifice has not been taken seriously since the Republic of China. This year, the Qinghai authorities felt the necessity of contacting the Mongolians and Tibetans because of the Yushu Incident. Therefore, Chairman Ma decided to participate in person in advance. The central government, feeling the importance of the Northwest, sent personnel to supervise, which has not happened in 21 years. The date of the sacrifice was originally scheduled for September 20, but was later changed to the 23rd because Chen Jingxiu, the representative of the central government, had not arrived, and Zhong Xingzai, the representative of the Xi'an Pacification Headquarters, only arrived in Xining on the 20th. The Mongolian banner princes, either participated in person, sent Taijis, or sent representatives, all gathered ahead of time. Many Tibetan tribal chiefs also participated. The princes in yellow jackets and white hats, and the tribal chiefs in red long sleeves, gathered together, with different costumes and different languages. However, a sense of cordiality overflowed from their brows. At 8 a.m. on the 23rd, the sea sacrifice ceremony was held at the Sea God Temple in Chahan City. The ceremony was quite grand.

After the sea sacrifice alliance meeting held in the past, a banquet should be held, and Dongquo Temple was used as the banquet venue. The temple is located in Tu'ergan, 60 miles from Chahan City. After the sea sacrifice this time, Chairman Ma ordered the translator to convey to the Mongolian and Tibetan princes and tribal chiefs to return to Dongquo Temple to gather for a banquet. At one time, they spurred their horses and galloped, vying to be the first. At 8 a.m. on the 24th, a banquet was set up in front of the sutra hall of Dongquo Temple. Chairman Ma, Representative Zhong, and Division Commander Ma and others sat in the middle seat, and the reporter also got a seat. The left side was the seat for the left-wing Mongolian chiefs and princes, the right side was the seat for the right-wing Mongolian chiefs and princes, and the lower side was the seat for the tribal chiefs. Small tables were set up on the ground. A raw sheep was placed in front of the upper table, and sugar, wine, and fruits were placed on the table. The rewards of Chairman Ma and Representative Zhong were also placed on the table. The seating arrangements and gifts were based on the level of status. In previous years, the tribal chiefs scrambled for seats, and the awards were given by calling out their names. This year, the principle of equality for all was adopted, and seats were set up for each. However, according to those familiar with the situation of the Mongolians and Tibetans, although this move was considered a great honor by the Tibetan people, the Mongolians were ashamed to be associated with the Tibetan people. However, in view of the current situation, the strength of the Tibetan tribal chiefs is indeed greater than that of the Mongolians. After sitting down, Chairman Ma led everyone to salute the portrait of the Prime Minister, and then the banquet began. During the banquet, Chairman Ma and Representative Zhong both gave earnest speeches on unity and resistance against foreign aggression. Finally, a banquet robbery was held. Fruits and mutton were placed in the courtyard. As soon as the master of ceremonies shouted the words "banquet robbery," everyone gathered in the courtyard, vying to be the first, pushing and shoving each other, and fighting fiercely. It is said in Qing customs that eating the food that is robbed will prevent illness for a year, so they are so enthusiastic. After the banquet, the princes and tribal chiefs ordered their servants to carry meat and wine, and carry gifts, and thanked Chairman Ma happily before leaving. This grand ceremony was completed. ㈡ Qinghai Politics Qinghai was the ancient Xiqiang. During the Qin Dynasty, it was called Huangzhong. Emperor Wu of the Han Dynasty drove away the various Qiang tribes and built new settlements. During the reign of Emperor Xuan of the Han Dynasty, Zhao Chongguo attacked the Xianling Qiang tribes and established Poqiang County, and garrisoned troops on the Huangshui River. The relics are still there today, reminding people of the work of developing the Northwest. The ancients also did it before us, but unfortunately, later generations could not continue it. During the Jian'an period of the Han Dynasty, Xiping County was established. At the end of the Eastern Jin Dynasty, Tuoba Wu, the prince of Southern Liang, occupied it as the capital. It was driven away by the Later Wei Dynasty. During the Sui Dynasty, the county was abolished. Liu Quan also garrisoned troops here. During the Tang Dynasty, it fell into Tubo. In the early Song Dynasty, it belonged to Western Xia, and later it was occupied by Tubo again. It was not until the Yuan Dynasty that it was called Xining, belonging to Gansu Province, and belonging to the Shaanxi Branch Secretariat. Mongolian tribes began to invade and live with the Tibetans. Some say that tens of thousands of Hui people also moved into Xining during the Hongwu period of the Ming Dynasty, but there is no proof. The Hui people in Xining, except for the Salar, mostly moved in during the Qing Dynasty. The Qing Dynasty pacified the Mongolians and Tibetans and changed it back to a prefecture. In the Republic of China, it was changed to a circuit. It was not until the winter of the 17th year that it was changed to Qinghai Province. Qinghai has a vast area. Yushu County is almost equal to Shaanxi Province. In addition, there are mixed ethnic groups, and there have been many rebellions. Taking Guoluo as an example, although Ma Xunchen led troops to conquer it the year before last, only the queen went to Xining, and the rest had nothing to do with it. However, the Ma family, father, son, uncle, and nephew, have a history of more than 30 years in Xining, and they are familiar with the situation. The results of their administration are not bad. At present, there are almost no bandits in the entire territory, and opium seedlings have disappeared. Prince Ziyuan, the director of the Civil Affairs Department, can adapt to the environment and work hard, so the civil affairs of Qinghai are still commendable. It is a pity that the ethnic groups are complex, and the Tibetan people have their own customs and regulations, which is inconvenient in judicial matters. Mongolian, Tibetan, and local ethnic groups have their own political systems, which often hinders administration. Even Jia Jia Ahong sometimes interferes in politics with religion. Although the provincial government has tried to improve this, it has not achieved significant results due to various restrictions. Although there was an agreement to integrate the local rulers into the regular administration, the local rulers still monopolize one side. Recently, the Civil Affairs Department plans to set up counties throughout the province and transform the princes and tribal chiefs into district chiefs, but it has not been implemented due to various reasons.

Overview of Machine Irrigation in Wuxi 79

Founded First by Xi Du Ding Biao

There are Now 2,000 Operating Machine Boats

A positive way to relieve rural areas is to start by improving agricultural tools. Electric irrigation in the Suxi area has proven effective, but since power plants are not yet widespread, the use of machine power instead of human and animal power is also worthy of attention. After investigating the irrigation area in Wuxi, a newspaper reporter took the opportunity to inquire about the status of machine drainage in Wuxi. The findings of the field visit are recorded below. The inventor of the water drainage machine was Ding Biao from Xiaoxuankou, Kaiyuan Township, Wuxi. Mr. Ding had never been engaged in industry. He was a farmer who also supplemented his income by raising fish. In the first year of the Xuantong reign of the Qing Dynasty, there was a major flood. When the fish ponds were full, there was concern of collapse. Drainage by people and animals was both slow and wasteful. In a state of anxiety day and night, he invented a machine to replace human and animal power. At first, he only hired workers to draw a sample and made a small-scale engine to drive the original waterwheel. After several improvements, he created a machine made purely of iron and steel. Since then, curious people have also imitated it, but society has not paid much attention to it. Only then did several farmers set up a machine on a boat in the nature of a company. In addition to self-use, they were also hired by others, and their profits were quite abundant. In the 14th and 15th years of the Republic, the weather was extremely dry, and human and animal power were exhausted and ineffective. Machine drainage became very effective. Water drainage machines are divided into diesel and kerosene types, and there are also kerosene and diesel dual-use types. The names are "horizontal diesel engine" ("vertical diesel engine"), "irrigation pump" (also known as "water wind box"), and "water drainage and rice milling dual-purpose machine," etc. The horsepower ranges from six to twelve, fourteen, sixteen, eighteen, and twenty-four horsepower. The price is calculated by horsepower. Diesel engines are 65 yuan per horsepower, and kerosene engines are 50 yuan. The most common is a 14-horsepower diesel engine. Including the boat, the total cost is 2,000 yuan, which farmers cannot directly afford to purchase. Machine boat operation has become an intermediate society. There are about 2,000 operating machine boats in the whole county. More than 1,310 boats have joined the association, and about 300 have not joined the association. In addition, they are scattered to neighboring counties. In the territory, districts 3, 5, 6, 11, 13, and 12 are the most common, all contracting fields according to value. This summer, due to the extreme drought, drainage day and night still caused losses to many. The average contracted price per mu is 1.8 yuan for high fields, 1.6 yuan for flat fields, and 1.4 yuan for low fields. The leading manufacturing factories are Gongyi, followed by Hezhong, and then Zhendan. There are more than 50 factories of various sizes, such as Xiangxing and Fuxing. The Model Irrigation Bureau organized by the Construction Committee once gathered pumps from factories in Shanghai, Wuxi, and Changzhou at the Changzhou First Irrigation Area for testing in the previous year. Gongyi's results were the best, and 100 units were ordered. Subsequently, the purchase reached 300 units. Last year, the Guangdong Construction Department also quickly purchased 50 units. In addition, they are also distributed in various provinces such as Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, Henan, and Shandong. Zhendan Factory was established later, but the owner has a strong enterprising spirit, and the products are getting better and better. They are sold in provinces such as Zhejiang, Sichuan, Anhui, and Guangdong. The factory has recently launched a new type of 7-horsepower light and convenient high-lift water pump, weighing only 600 pounds net, equipped with a 4-inch diameter pump, which can discharge 220 gallons of water per minute. Equipped with a 5-inch diameter pump, it can discharge 350 gallons of water per minute. Its uses are not limited to drainage. It can also be used for engineering drainage, building high water towers, firefighting, power generation, and rice milling. Other various machine parts can also be driven by it. Local Communication

Meeting on Custody of Land Survey Fees: This county has been ordered to prepare for the establishment of a Land Bureau to collect and store land survey fees for future surveys. Previously, the provincial order was to collect land survey fees calculated by the mu, but after local agencies fought for it, it was handled according to the land value tax collection. Now, the collection of this land survey fee has begun. The committee members for the custody of land survey fees, which should be established according to regulations, were established yesterday. During the discussion of the agenda, County Chief Shen chaired the meeting. ㈠ Chairman Shen submitted a proposal to designate an institution to store the collected land survey fees. It was resolved to store them in the county's Farmers Bank according to regulations. ㈠ Chairman Shen submitted a proposal to recommend committee members to be in charge of the custody committee seal awarded by the provincial government. It was resolved that Committee Member Shen should be in charge of it. ㈡ Chairman Shen submitted a proposal on how to recommend the standing committee members of the committee. It was resolved that, in addition to the Director of the Finance Bureau as a member by default, Committee Member Shen and Committee Member Cha were recommended as standing committee members. ㈠ Chairman Shen submitted a proposal on how to stipulate the procedures for collecting, depositing, and withdrawing land survey fees. It was resolved that A. The two cabinets should report the collected land survey fees to the Finance Bureau at any time. The Finance Bureau should fill out a three-part remittance slip and transfer it to the committee for verification and collection. A return receipt should be issued for filing. B. The committee should deposit the funds collected by the Finance Bureau into the designated county Farmers Bank immediately. C. Withdrawals should be approved by the Provincial Land Bureau and a check should be issued. The committee should affix the seal of the standing committee members to withdraw the funds. ㈠ Chairman Shen submitted a proposal on whether the date of the monthly regular meeting of the committee should be stipulated. It was resolved that the meeting should be held at 10:00 a.m. on the 15th of each month.

Court Trial Record of the Xiecheng Pawnshop Lawsuit: The Lou Tang Xiecheng Pawnshop claimed that the pawned items were lost during the looting in the war, and those with an original pawn value of one yuan were only refunded six cents. Only the head ornaments were. According to the defendant, they were transported to the Jiading Jiping Pawnshop for deposit and storage, which led to the loss. Therefore, the pawnshop should be responsible. Please order the court to redeem the items according to the pawn ticket. Xiang Jian'an confessed that he was the manager of Xiecheng. The clothes were transported to Shanghai and were slightly lost, estimated at hundreds of yuan. He also submitted a list of losses. Witness Xuan Bao confessed that during the war, he traveled with Wang Xiaoshan from Waigang, transporting the pawned items of Xiecheng Pawnshop to Shanghai. There were no losses along the way. Ministry of Education Promulgates Measures for Service and Treatment of Faculty and Staff in Secondary Schools 92

The Ministry of Education issues a circular to the Education Bureaus of all provinces and cities, stating: The purpose of secondary education is, on the one hand, to cultivate healthy citizens and make them the backbone of society, and on the other hand, to cultivate the foundation of higher education and prepare them for employment. Its importance is closely related to all levels of education. At present, the effectiveness of secondary education in our country is still quite limited. The reasons are certainly manifold, but the unsuitability of school administration and the neglect of student discipline are the most important factors. These are discussed separately below.

The sole aim of all facilities in school administration is to improve the efficiency of education. Given the difficulties of education in various parts of our country, school facilities must carefully weigh priorities and adopt the most economical and effective methods. Today, principals of secondary schools in various places do not teach and resemble the heads of administrative organs. Teachers are paid by the hour, and their salaries are often meager. They fear that their teaching hours are insufficient. They have no leisure to further their studies, and their salaries are insufficient to support their families. In terms of administrative affairs, officials are appointed indiscriminately, public funds are wasted, teachers' salaries cannot be raised, and facilities cannot be established. This kind of malpractice is especially prevalent in public schools. If we want to improve the efficiency of education, but instead hinder and stagnate it, this is the first thing that urgently needs improvement.

In recent years, the academic atmosphere of secondary schools has declined, and the blame is generally placed on the mismanagement of discipline. However, the real problem is the lack of suitable personnel. Since the implementation of the system of paying teachers by the hour, its most negative impact has been that anything outside of class time is not the teacher's responsibility. The important task of discipline is entrusted to the so-called discipline personnel, who are generally less qualified and unable to honestly teach. Students have little faith in them, and even good regulations are difficult to enforce. Over time, school rules are disregarded, and various bad behaviors arise. Their thoughts and feelings are further dominated by the trends of the times, and their innate qualities react in an unrestrained manner. Education's power to change temperament and overcome the environment is completely lost. Those who are teachers should take it as their duty to establish themselves and others. It is not just about teaching and resolving doubts. Today's teachers only limit themselves to teaching knowledge and do not bear the heavy responsibility of discipline. This makes students only know that going to school is solely for acquiring knowledge, and nothing else matters. Over time, the academic atmosphere cannot but decline. This is the second thing that urgently needs improvement.

The Ministry has specially formulated the Outline of Measures for Service and Treatment of Faculty and Staff in Secondary Schools, which are hereby issued to all concerned. In terms of school administration, we will strive for rationalization and economization. Salaries that have been wasted on faculty and staff in the past, except for hourly wages, will be used to increase teachers' salaries. School affairs will be assigned to teachers, and the spirit of teachers assisting the principal in governing the school together will be realized. In terms of student discipline, we will strive to eliminate the previous drawbacks of separating discipline from teaching, so that all teachers bear the responsibility of discipline. The principal will designate some teachers to concurrently take charge of discipline, establishing the foundation of character education. However, given the vast territory of our country and the different conditions in various places, the salary grades of faculty and staff in secondary schools in each province and city, the assignment of school affairs to teachers, and the concurrent assignment of discipline matters should be promptly formulated separately by the bureaus in accordance with local conditions and based on this outline, and reported to the Ministry for approval. It is expected that from the next semester, the discipline measures of secondary schools nationwide can be corrected. From the next school year, the education salary measures will also be uniformly revised, so that the efficiency of secondary education will be enhanced and the entire education system will be promoted. All bureaus should strictly comply with these instructions and forward them to their subordinates for compliance. This order includes a copy of the Outline of Measures for Service and Treatment of Faculty and Staff in Secondary Schools.

Outline of Measures for Service and Treatment of Faculty and Staff in Secondary Schools 93

1. Secondary schools should be jointly governed by faculty and staff, assisted by the principal. All school administration and discipline matters should be handled separately by the principal's appointed full-time teachers and part-time educators.

2. Secondary schools shall abolish the hourly wage system. The monthly salaries of faculty and staff shall be graded and advanced in order. Part-time teachers may be paid by the hour. All provinces and bureaus shall stipulate regulations based on local living standards and better current practices.

3. All provinces and cities shall make every effort to promote the annual salary increase system and the measures stipulated in the regulations on teacher and staff retirement pensions and survivor benefits.

4. The in-class teaching time for full-time teachers in junior high schools shall be 22 to 26 hours per week, and the in-class teaching time for full-time teachers in senior high schools shall be 20 to 24 hours per week. If there are special circumstances in various places that require an increase, both senior and junior high schools may increase the amount as appropriate.

5. The principal of a secondary school must undertake teaching, and the time must not be less than one-half of the minimum teaching time of a full-time teacher, and no separate salary shall be paid.

6. The teaching time for the director of academic affairs and the director of student affairs may be reduced as appropriate for full-time teachers, but must not be less than two-thirds of the prescribed minimum. If there is a director of general affairs, the teaching time should also be determined according to this regulation.

7. If the number of teaching hours in a subject in a secondary school is sufficient for the prescribed number of hours for a full-time teacher, or if the number of teaching hours in a subject is insufficient, and the number of hours in other subjects with similar properties is combined to reach the prescribed number of hours for a full-time teacher, a full-time teacher should be hired immediately.

8. The number of part-time teachers in a school shall not exceed one-fifth of the total number of teachers. Part-time teachers shall be limited to the three subjects of music, drawing, and manual arts in principle.

9. Full-time teachers are absolutely not allowed to hold concurrent positions outside the school.

10. Full-time teachers must share the responsibility of guiding students' extracurricular self-study. Part-time teachers should also guide students' extracurricular self-study once or twice a week.

11. The principal and all teachers must bear the responsibility of discipline. The full-time positions such as director of student affairs and discipline officers must be held concurrently by full-time teachers.

12. Full-time teachers who concurrently hold positions such as academic affairs and discipline should be paid a higher monthly salary.

13. In addition to the use of specialists for accounting and general affairs, and for matters such as writing, secondary schools may use a very small number of clerks and secretaries, and must not indiscriminately establish any official positions.

14. If necessary for practical reasons, secondary vocational schools may use a very small number of related technical assistants.

...enters the Yangtze River. This is truly a critical moment for China's survival. All citizens should be vigilant. However, the Japanese have been plotting against us for a long time. Since the Meiji Restoration, several decades have passed. During that time, they have reformed their politics, revitalized their industries, and strengthened their military. From top to bottom, they have done everything. Now, they have unleashed their accumulated strength to seize our rich territory as easily as taking something from a pocket. The major powers are watching with concern, but are helpless. The League of Nations is mediating, but they turn a deaf ear, relying on their strength and showing no fear. Their flames are especially fierce. China is a great nation with a vast territory of four million square miles, a population of 400 to 500 million, and abundant resources, the richest in the world. Why is it so weak that it cannot resist the invasion of the dwarfs? It is because the people are afraid of difficulties, seek ease, lack creativity, and lack the spirit of old fighters. This is why. In the past, Baden-Powell, who was stationed in South Africa, saw that the indigenous people of Africa used their own strength for everything they ate, wore, and did, and they had a spirit of hard work and struggle. So he took their way of life and created the Boy Scouts. Material civilization is improving day by day, with tall buildings and mansions, light furs and warm robes, and delicacies from land and sea. What place does not have them? But the Boy Scouts must build their own tents, live in remote wilderness, and hunt animals, wearing coarse clothes and carrying sticks. Is this contrary to the path of evolution? It is also to cultivate their spirit of enduring hardship, hard work, struggle, and creativity in preparation for serving the country and society. Only after a fierce wind do we know the strength of the grass; only after hardship do we see the spirit. This is why Boy Scout education is valued by all countries in the world. Today, the urgent task of our country is to recover the lost territory of the three northeastern provinces. However, there must be a way to recover the lost territory. Just shouting and complaining is of no help. In the past, King Goujian of Yue did not forget the shame of Kuaiji. He slept on brushwood and tasted gall, gathering strength and training for twenty years to defeat Wu. This Jiangsu Provincial Secondary School Boy Scout Grand Encampment lasts for three days, which is a short time. However, it is hoped that all boy scouts will uphold this spirit, never lose it, endure hardship, sacrifice, and struggle, study hard, and serve society. If we always keep in mind the great revenge, then with China's abundant natural resources and the strength of its people, the recovery of the lost territory can be expected soon. Let us all strive for it.

New Basketball Techniques (20) 7

(Not Allowed) Original author: Clair Burcky (Reprint) Translated and explained by Zhang Guodong and Qian Yiquan

The most important aspects of this tactic are the bounce pass, quick scoring, agile decoy, and skillful turning, etc. This method is now widely used in the school playgrounds of Indiana, USA. It is often used as a strategy for attacking zone defenses and five-man zone defenses.

Number one rushes out from the corner of his own court, running towards the free-throw area. He receives a bounce pass from number four. Numbers three and five feint to move forward to the right front, but after attracting their defenders to the right, they turn and head to the left. Number five runs to the arc of the free-throw area and receives a pass from number one, then immediately passes it to number three, who is charging towards the basket. At this time, if number one's defender blocks number three, then number two can find a way to move forward to the basket to receive number three's pass.
