Jiang Jiao Reappears at the 6-Qian Level 175

| Small Profit, Peaceful Market |

Yesterday was Sunday, and banks were closed as usual. Although money shops operated normally, business procedures were inevitably reduced. The market price of foreign cents did not change due to the lack of competition. The morning market was at 7 qian, 0 li, 7 hao, 3 si, 7 hu, and half a xian, the same price as the previous noon. The afternoon market was slightly softer by 125, at 7 qian, 0 li, 7 hao, and 2 hao and a half. Transactions were made. Morning market exchange settlement was 285,000, and banknotes were 20,000. Afternoon market exchange settlement was 180,000, and banknotes were 15,000. The silver discount for both morning and afternoon markets was 4%. Money shops collected and transferred over 4.4 million foreign yuan, silver shops collected and transferred over 19 million, various routes collected over 400,000, and discount ticket transactions were over 5 million. Small money shop transactions were over 300,000. The exchange rate for Jiangnan small foreign coins in both morning and afternoon markets was 6 qian, 1 fen, 2 li, and half a xian. Transactions were only 4,500 jiao in the morning market. The Guangdong small foreign coin market was 5 qian, 9 fen, 9 li, 7 hao, and half a xian in the morning market. The market opened at 6 qian, a half a li better than the previous market. Transactions were 75,000 jiao in the morning market and 45,000 jiao in the afternoon market. Copper coins were 418,500 wen, an increase of 500 wen compared to the previous day.

Securities Bonds Slightly Up Last Week 176

| Trend Gradually Stabilizing, Very Stagnant on Weekends |

| Total Turnover of Over 25 Million for the Whole Week |

The bond market situation of the Chinese Business Securities Exchange from October 31st to November 5th last week showed that the spot trading volume was higher than the previous week. Most bonds were actively traded, with a total turnover of 122,000 yuan for the whole week, including 40,000 yuan for salt tax bonds, and around 13,000 yuan each for demobilization, 20-customs, 19-customs, and financial bonds. Full six and demobilization bonds were about 9,000 yuan. Other transactions were less active. In the futures market, the price settlement rose at the beginning of the week, and trading was very active. The market sentiment was very lively, with weekly trading reaching 7.8 million. Tuesday also had 5.5 million yuan. Afterward, it gradually calmed down. From Wednesday to Friday, the daily turnover was around 3 million yuan. The weekend was very slow, with only 1.8 million yuan. Statistics for the whole week show a total turnover of 25,140,000 yuan, an increase of over 4 million yuan compared to the previous week. Among them, unified salt tax bonds were the most active, with 4.93 million yuan for November contracts and 10,000 yuan for December contracts. Unified tax bonds had 30,000 yuan for December contracts and 4.14 million yuan for November contracts. Demobilization and 20-customs bonds followed. Demobilization bonds had 2,375,000 yuan for November contracts and 1,485,000 yuan for December contracts. 20-customs bonds had 3,230,000 yuan for November contracts and 15,000 yuan for December contracts. 20-series bonds had 2,785,000 yuan for November contracts and 45,000 yuan for December contracts. Others also performed better than before. 19-customs bonds had 1,790,000 yuan for November contracts and 35,000 yuan for December contracts. 19-series bonds had 1,455,000 yuan for November contracts and 10,000 yuan for December contracts. Demobilization bonds had 1,430,000 yuan for November contracts and 5,000 yuan for December contracts. Customs bonds for the next month had 710,000 yuan. Full six bonds for the next month had 415,000 yuan. 96 public bonds had 145,000 yuan. Financial bonds had 10,000 yuan. In addition, the total for November contracts of various bonds was 23.4 million, but December contracts were only 1.74 million. Regarding the price trend of various bonds last week, it has been slightly more stable than the previous week, and daily fluctuations were uncertain, rising and falling suddenly. There was no consistent trend, indicating that the price increase of various bonds is gradually coming to an end. The domestic and international situation did not see major developments during this period. The bond market environment was more dull than before, and market sentiment was increasingly cautious. Therefore, the first two days of the week were generally active, but later became more idle. On Monday, only full six and demobilization bonds rose by more than one yuan, and other bonds did not change significantly. On Tuesday, there were mutual gains and losses, with fluctuations of only a few jiao. Wednesday saw a slight decrease of one or two jiao. Thursday saw gains of three or four jiao to seven or eight jiao. The weekend saw a slight contraction, but the amount was small. As a result, demobilization, full six, and financial bonds continued to rise by one yuan and four or five jiao compared to the previous week. However, many spot goods rose significantly, mainly due to the removal of principal and interest from the previous period. Looking at the future of the bond market, it will return to calmness. If the environment does not change, the market is unlikely to develop before mid-month. Yarn and Cotton Flower: Yarn Market Declines Last Week 177

| "Ren" Character Hits New Low |

Cotton yarn prices fell sharply last week due to the recovery of overseas cotton markets and sluggish domestic demand. The tight financial situation affected all groups, making them unable to procure supplies. Consequently, spot yarn business was quite quiet. Currently, Japanese merchants are dumping large quantities of Japanese yarn in the Yangtze River region, impacting local yarn prices. Although this year's harvest is plentiful in the Gengsi countryside, low prices for agricultural products have made life difficult for the villagers, resulting in weak purchasing power. As a result, most speculators are actively selling off their holdings. At the same time, some manufacturers are very willing to sell "Ren" character, ship, and cotton flower yarns, and are willing to compromise on prices. Therefore, sellers have abundant inventory. Although Wing On speculators are still struggling to hold on, the environment is too bad, and the trend is unstoppable, leading to new lows in the market. Later in the week, American cotton prices rose slightly, prompting profit-takers to cover their short positions, slightly increasing market conditions. As for yarn sales to Sichuan, the war is ongoing, and purchases have not started. There are occasional purchases of long-term futures from old customers. Business from other regions is quite slow. A total of 7,279 bales were purchased by various groups throughout the week, with "Zhong" character goods accounting for the majority. Standard yarn speculators have closed their positions, and prices for each month have fallen by 2 taels and 14 qian compared to the previous week. Total turnover for the week was 129,650 bales. The volume of cotton being sold by a certain manufacturer is increasing, adding to the pressure. As a result, the market is difficult to reverse, and sentiment is unanimously bearish. Midway through the week, the slight fall in gold prices triggered a sudden plunge in the market, reaching new lows. The low price for November delivery was once seen at 29 taels and 7 qian and a half. Hunan Xiangxian Cargo to Arrive in Shanghai Soon 182

Yesterday, the foreign rice market was completely stagnant. As river rice prices fell, the street had no further use for it. Customers disliked the price, and there was no inquiry from actual consumers. Therefore, it was quiet all day, and there were no transactions in the overall market. Fuzhou groups still had a strong appetite, but they were paying attention to the Ke Xian rice, and had no interest in foreign rice. The previously arrived Xiang-Gan Ke Xian rice had all been purchased by this group, and recent stocks had run out. There was a gap in the new supply, so there were no transactions yesterday. However, two batches of Hunan rice have been loaded and are on their way, the first batch of about four or five hundred bags, will arrive today or tomorrow. It is expected that the Fuzhou group will take most of the supply when it arrives, as the North group is taking a wait-and-see attitude, and the street has no intention of intervening, it is said.

There were no transactions in tinplate, corrugated iron, small Guangzhou leather, red gang leather, new lead, etc., and there were no changes in price levels either.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Speech

Wearing High Hats 194

— Fo

｜Five of the Art of Living｜

Wearing high hats is flattery, and people who like to wear high hats are, after all, willing to admit it. This is generally common psychology. The so-called "Thousands of wears, ten thousand wears, flattery never wears out," but there are also differences. Some people know that others are giving me a high hat, and pretend not to know. Some people wear high hats themselves and are still clueless, which is truly pitiful.

Cao Cao was truly a treacherous villain. Sun Guan once sent him a high hat, and he knew it. In the twenty-fourth year of Emperor Xian of Han, Sun Guan submitted a memorial, claiming allegiance to Cao, and speaking of the Mandate of Heaven. Cao showed it to outsiders, saying, "Is this child trying to put me on the stove?" At that time, Chen Qun and several other ministers were all doing favors and desperately sending high hats to Cao Cao, saying, "Your Highness's merits are towering, you should assume the great position." Cao said, "If the Mandate of Heaven is with me, I will be King Wen of Zhou." He ultimately refused to wear this high hat, which was his cleverness.

But some people wear high hats themselves and still don't realize it, which is truly laughable. The "Sayings of Master Lianchi" states, "In the past, an old monk said, 'There is no one in the world who does not like fame,' and then sighed deeply. One person in the audience stood up and asked, 'Indeed, as you say, is the only one who does not like fame?' The old monk was very happy, not knowing that a high hat had been gently placed on his head. He was still pleased with himself. From this, we can see that if someone offers you a high hat, it is very difficult to completely refuse it.

My poetry is completely unrefined, and I can't do it well, and I don't even know when I've lost rhyme. Because of the words "high hat," I once wrote a crooked poem. No matter what, I'll write it below for the readers to have a laugh. On the Lantern Festival, a friend gave me a Western hat and wrote, "I offer you a high hat as a New Year's greeting for prosperity and good fortune." I sang it as a joke:

I am grateful for your gift of a high hat,

Bright and dazzling, beyond compare.

I ask, from where did this object come?

You spent a fortune to buy it in the market.

There are so many high hats here,

Even a stubborn person like you has one.

How elegant are the caps and belts in the world,

Carriages follow each other in extravagance.

I am just a cooking dog butcher,

A monkey in a hat, shaming the country.

I tell the snobs of the world,

Don't let Zhang wear Li's hat.

Literature and Art

Ode to the League of Nations and the Investigation Team 195

— Xu Lige

In the past, the League of Nations was majestic,

But it has not stopped the fierce tigers and wolves.

How many weak and small sympathize with me,

The rabbit dies, the fox grieves, and resentment is unbearable.

Resulting in unfair joint control,

What is left for a thousand years to judge?

Such a large institution has lost its credibility,

Relying on an empty city as a Great Wall is absurd.

The old and still romantic Lord Lytton,

His spirit was ultimately sacrificed in vain.

Truly knowing the result would be like this,

He regrets welcoming them at the time. (In return)

Science

Method for Manufacturing By-products During Salt Production 196

— Department Heart

When manufacturing table salt, regardless of the method used, a large amount of bittern is inevitably produced, hence it is a by-product of salt production. It tastes bitter, is a yellow oily liquid with a specific gravity of 1.20-1.28. Besides the remaining table salt, its main components are magnesium chloride and magnesium sulfate, and it also contains small amounts of chlorides, sulfates, and bromide iodides. Therefore, it can be used to produce magnesium sulfate and magnesium carbonate, and the method is as follows:

(1) Method for Producing Magnesium Sulfate: Because magnesium sulfate is not easily dissolved in a liquid containing a large amount of magnesium chloride, this effect can be used to place the bittern in the refrigerator. In the cold of winter, magnesium sulfate will crystallize and precipitate as translucent crystals.

Then, add hot clean water to a pot to reach about 70 degrees, and gradually add the impure magnesium sulfate crystals, stirring to dissolve them. Stop adding when the specific gravity of the mother liquor reaches 36 degrees, and let it stand to settle the mixed impurities. After about 10 hours, filter it through a sand filter, and the temperature must be maintained between 50 and 60 degrees at this time. Cool the filtrate, and magnesium sulfate crystals will precipitate on the liquid surface at a temperature of about 10 degrees. If the obtained crystals are not good, use a sprayer to spray dew-like water to thin the surface, and crystals will precipitate from the lower layer. After the crystals are completely formed, take them out and dry them to obtain refined magnesium sulfate. Because the remaining residual liquid still contains a small amount of magnesium sulfate, it can be mixed into the next batch of liquid to continue crystallization. After three or four times, the residual liquid contains many impurities and can be discarded. Usually, about 70 pounds of pure magnesium sulfate can be obtained from 100 pounds of impure magnesium sulfate. The crystals are prismatic or needle-like crystals, soluble in twice their weight of water, and the solution should be neutral. Adding silver nitrate will not produce a white precipitate, and adding ammonium carbonate will also not produce a precipitate. The above-mentioned properties are usually used to identify whether magnesium sulfate is pure. It is the well-known Epsom salt in medicine and can also be used as fertilizer and in dyeing. It can also be used to make soap.

The territory has been lost, and most of it is still dancing. If they do not wake up early, they will be caught in one net.

(2) Method for Producing Magnesium Carbonate: After the magnesium sulfate crystals are precipitated from the bittern, the remaining liquid still contains a large amount of magnesium chloride. Although this substance can be made into pure products, it has no value, so it is now used to make magnesium carbonate.

The method is to filter the bittern after the magnesium sulfate is precipitated through sand and use a Baume hydrometer to measure its specific gravity. Then, dissolve sodium carbonate in water to make its specific gravity equal to that of the bittern, let it stand for two hours to precipitate impurities, and then slowly inject it into the bittern, stirring it. The reaction will produce magnesium carbonate precipitate. The temperature should be maintained at around 60 degrees at this time. The amount of magnesium carbonate solution added should be 62.3% of the bittern. After completely adding it, let it stand for one or two hours, then add a little more sodium carbonate solution. If no precipitate continues to form, it can be filtered. Take the precipitate and put it in a washing tank. This tank is a rectangular wooden trough with a depth of two feet six inches, a length of six feet, and a width of four feet. There is a drainage outlet at the bottom, and the tank is filled with two or three inches of sand particles, covered with a piece of cloth. After the magnesium carbonate is transferred in, slowly inject clean water to wash it for about 20 hours to remove sulfates and chlorides. Then, wrap it in cloth to remove its moisture and dry it to obtain pure magnesium carbonate. Approximately one stone and five dou of bittern plus 180 pounds of sodium carbonate can yield 100 pounds of magnesium carbonate. It is a white, odorless, loose powder that can be completely dissolved in 50 times its weight of dilute nitric acid. Adding magnesium nitrate and silver nitrate will not produce a white precipitate. If one part of magnesium carbonate is added to 20 parts of distilled water, the liquid is filtered and evaporated to dryness, it will not produce a large amount of precipitate. These properties are usually used to identify the quality of magnesium carbonate. It can be used to make fire bricks and hard building materials, so it is often used in building construction.

Society Improvement Discussion Group

The So-called (Improving Children) 197

— Xinshan

In China, (children) have always been neglected, and everyone has regarded them as unimportant. But today, it has become a serious problem. Many educators have completely shifted their focus in this direction, dedicating their entire bodies to this cause! Because children are like the young sprouts of plants, if education is improper in this era, it is easy to submerge their pure nature and destroy their immature minds. In the future, they will grow up to be nothing more than disabled beings unfit for society!

Children are the foundation of the country. Can we heartlessly allow their nature to be submerged, their minds to be destroyed, and thus lead the country to ruin?·······

For these reasons, I have read Mr. Feifei's so-called (Improving Children) article. I read it again and again, and it greatly stirred my interest in this issue. I would like to say something that doesn't quite fit in. Fortunately, our Mr. Feifei has added a tail to the end of his article: "What do the editors think? What do the members of this association and the readers think?" As a small reader (I really dare not, and am not worthy to be called Mr. Feifei's colleague), I respectfully accept this opportunity to say what I want to say.

Mr. Feifei's long, 900-word article on what children urgently need to (improve) lists ten items: (1) Children must decide their own (color) of clothes, decide their own (style), and decide their own (material); (2) Clothes must (not be too tight) and (not be too loose); (3) Clothes must not be worn too warmly

Page 16

or too coolly; (4) Clothes must be worn neatly and completely, and the family must have a dressing mirror, a clothes rack, and a clothes brush···· Unfortunately, I cannot fully introduce it here, please readers turn to the old newspaper to appreciate it themselves. In short, Mr. Feifei has exhausted his mind and spent much effort thinking about (improving) children's (clothing and footwear). He can truly be called an angel for children! (Clothing and footwear) expert!

But (angels) are nothing but religious people's lies to deceive fools and earn their own living! (Angels) will never truly benefit children! Our Mr. Feifei has also made a mistake! Alas! Alas, our Mr. Feifei has also made a mistake!

We are extremely saddened by the extravagance of modern people! We are extremely distressed by modern people's obsession with fashion! Extravagance and fashion are things for young ladies and young masters, but can (young ladies) and (young masters) save the country from its difficulties? We are precisely distressed by the fact that there are so many young ladies and young masters in our declining China, and we are still madly manufacturing more? None of the ten items that Mr. Feifei calls good is anything other than wanting to make every child dress up as neatly and elegantly as a young master or young lady. Dressing neatly, fetching rice and pouring water, and calling for servants to stand around? Apart from this, with their pure nature submerged and their immature minds destroyed, what good is there? As for dressing mirrors, clothes racks, clothes brushes, etc., even I, who can barely hold a pen to write, would not meet Mr. Feifei's criteria even if I starved for a week: I don't know about other people's homes.

Our children are like this, Mr. Feifei, please listen to my song:

(Our) children, wear clothes made of old cloth,

Splattered with mud,

The sleeves and trouser legs are always rolled high to the elbows and knees, and sometimes they go barefoot to the fields with hoes;

Sometimes they go to the threshing ground with axes and saws;

They also read books, sing songs, and go to school.

(Our) children are truly the pillars of society, the beams of the country!

School Scene

The Barber 198

— Xianhuang

Clang, clang, clang... the class bell rang, and the geography teacher, nicknamed "The Barber," walked slowly into the classroom.

"Teacher, hello!" Li said with a very comical tone.

"Li, calm down, no shouting in class," the geography teacher said sternly.

"Teacher, you're too intolerant, how can you scold people?" Zhu said, appearing to be defending Li. "Zhu, don't be nosy, or I'll be rude," the teacher said, his face turning red as he scolded Zhu.

"Teacher, why are you called a barber?" Li asked with a smile.

"Li, have you prepared your lesson?" The geography teacher pretended to be deaf as he asked Li.

"Ask away! At most, I'll get a zero," Li replied with a smile.

"What is the name of the largest island in Asia?"

"Teacher, a razor blade!"

"Ha..." Many classmates couldn't help but laugh.

"Li, do you want to continue studying?" The geography teacher's face turned white with anger.

"Hey! That's strange! If I didn't want to continue studying, I wouldn't have come long ago!"

"You are truly a little hooligan."

"Teacher, then you are an old geezer, right?"

"Bastard! Get out!"

"Get out? I won't get out."

"Get out!" The geography teacher, with a stern face, ran down from the podium and tried to pull Li.

"Let go! I don't need you to pull me."

Clang, clang, clang... the class bell rang, and the geography teacher had no choice but to swallow his anger and leave the classroom.

"The Barber..." strange calls continued. (In return)

Nonsense

The Three Contradictions of Modern Women 199

— Xuebiao

The term "modern woman" is all the rage in modern society, but since I became aware of this term, I have discovered many contradictions in them. Now, let me tell you about them:

(1) When we look at ordinary modern women, their hair is as long as ten thousand black snakes, and we can often see long hair hanging down their shoulders like Louis XIV's. Some part it in the middle with a pale white line and comb it into two thick and short braids on both sides. Some perm it into stiff hedgehog-like spikes, which may be said to be the most fashionable. But what is the difference between this and the braids and buns of the past? The purpose of cutting hair is for fashion, hygiene, convenience, saving time, and practicality, but now, changing to long hair is considered fashionable, and the time spent is about the same as before when keeping long hair. What is the point of this? So, this is one of their contradictions.

(2) Looking again at the clothes of ordinary modern women, let's take the cheongsam as an example. From cheongsams with wide sleeves and long hems to cheongsams with wide sleeves and short hems, and then to cheongsams with narrow sleeves and long hems, the styles are ever-changing. The most fashionable cheongsams now have sleeves that are short to above the elbows and so narrow that they cling to the arms. And the length of the dress? It is so long that it drags on the ground even when wearing high heels, exposing a large section of fair arms to attract attention. This is Europeanization. Just like skirts dragging on the ground in the past, it is only fifty steps compared to a hundred steps with Chinese traditional customs! So, this is their second contradiction.

(3) Finally, let's appreciate their feet! High-heeled shoes are the most European thing possible! Modern women always need them, but foreign women wear the same high-heeled shoes very differently. They have a healthy gait. When Chinese women wear them, they move with delicate steps and give a feeling of being too weak to withstand the wind. What is the difference between this and the bound feet of the past? It really makes people wonder where the beauty lies. This is their third contradiction.

After saying a lot above, I can summarize it in one sentence: I think that modern women, besides beauty, should pay attention to being convenient for action and operation, because they are singing loudly about women's liberation. Then, shouldn't they use their strength to fight for it? Of course, they can't be like the young ladies of the past, who would fall over in the wind! And they can't have three servants and four maids to support them, but now they are wearing gourd-shaped cheongsams and a pair of high-heeled shoes that resemble bound feet. Don't mention working, even walking is like a wobbly tumbler, so I say they are not worthy of being modern women. Truly modern women are the girls in the countryside who are qualified. I will frankly and impolitely call these fake modern women contradictory women!

Movie Special Edition Monday, November 7, 1932, Republic of China

Overseas News

Clara Bow's New Career 202

— Kang Bing

The new Clara Bow has long forgotten the former Clara Bow, and she hopes Hollywood will also forget her. Because people generally say she is making a "comeback," but Clara herself claims this is the beginning of her "new career," not a "comeback," let alone a "return to the screen."

This is a new beginning. The past indulgences only serve as a reminder for the current Clara. She has now completely changed her demeanor and views. The new Clara Bow is a mature and accomplished actress. Her childishness has disappeared, and she has now become a dignified and capable actress.

She now has a new house. She told people, "From now on, I will observe the new trends in Hollywood from this window." It is not because the old house on Peveley Hill was not suitable, but because it gave her many bad memories and images.

She is now an actress with Fox Film Corporation. The Fox decorators were extremely concerned about her dressing room. They first inquired about her dressing room at Paramount Pictures, which was completely decorated in black and gold. So, they also planned to paint her new dressing room in black and gold. But when the new Clara heard about this plan, she sincerely thanked the decorators for their sincerity, but requested that green and white colors be used instead.

The purpose of her "new career" is certainly to make money, but before she decided to shoot "Call Her Savage," she had considered the scripts proposed by various companies and her own role. She finally accepted the contract from Fox Film Corporation. (It is said that she will be paid 125,000 gold dollars for each film.)

Reader Opinions

What Kind of Movies Do We Need? 204

— Jizhong

Everyone, you don't think that movies are the only tool for entertainment, do you? Undoubtedly, they have the important task of raising people's knowledge, promoting national culture, reforming society, and improving everything. Especially, we can believe that the trends and styles of movies in any country are related to the lifeline of the entire country. Facts are powerful proof, and I will write down some of the more obvious ones here.

(1) The trend of American movies is that they always carry a display of splendor and magnificence, fully showing the atmosphere of singing, dancing, and prosperity. With a lot of money, American movies can never get rid of the color of extravagance and waste, that is, ideal movies, artistic movies, and aristocratic movies. On the one hand, they also specialize in depicting and inserting the love between men and women and the private affairs of romance as necessary. The whole of America is also in the microcosm of movies.

(2) Japan's film industry is indeed still immature and not as good as ours, but in terms of consciousness and reason, they are undoubtedly much superior to us. They do not make supernatural movies such as flying swords and fighting magic to anesthetize the entire society. At the same time, they do not shoot erotic and romantic movies to poison young men and women. Bushido is their standard for shooting movies, encouraging the greatness of war, promoting the spirit of fighting. Killing is their entire way out. Thus, people's consciousness and concepts are fully affected by the movies. One hundred and twenty percent unreasonable invasion of China's Northeast, but the people still shouted loudly, willing to be the backing. Although the reasons for this are very complicated, the impact created by the art of film also accounts for an important part.

(With national disasters approaching and national affairs becoming increasingly difficult,) our film industry should take some responsibility. Then, we should swear that we will never again shoot movies of licentiousness, theft, absurdity, gods, demons, or romance. What we need are movies that are realistic and not ideal, diligent and thrifty and not extravagant, active and not passive, brave and not decadent. At the same time, they are resistant and not non-resistant, and the spirit of fighting and killing is even more indispensable as a background. The movie industry, which is like an ox, can wake up.

The Second Chinese Movie Star? 205

— Zhenhua

Translated from Film Pictorial

The first Chinese movie star in the American film industry was Ms. Anna May Wong, who was already highly respected by American filmmakers. Now, continuing after Ms. Wong, the second Chinese movie star is Toshi Mori (transliteration). She already has a good reputation in the United States and has now signed a five-year contract with Columbia Pictures.

She is only nineteen years old. Although she was born in Kyoto, she grew up in the United States. She was discovered in Chinatown in the United States, because Columbia Pictures was looking for a Chinese actress to play a role in the film *The Bitter Tea of General Yen*. Therefore, they gave her a temporary contract. After the filming was completed, they signed a new five-year contract.

She said it was very sudden, because she had not been able to find a job for two years. During that time, no one noticed her. She thought she was going to fail, but suddenly Columbia noticed her. She is truly extremely lucky.

This (Chinese movie star)’s name is Toshi Mori. Isn't that a name that is living proof of sharing our (race and culture)? And she was born in Kyoto. Is that Kyoto (Japan)? Our national power in China is so weak, would we still try to pass off their nationality as ours? This is a bit strange. - Editor's Note

Joan Crawford Loves Tranquility 206

—

Louis Milestone's opinion: Joan Crawford's performance in *Rain* was the best, because that film was shot on Catalina Island. There were not as many friends or visitors watching her as on an ordinary set. In reality, she is a neurotic and shy woman, and she hates having people surrounding her and watching her. Therefore, when filming her, it is best to have no one except the necessary staff and cameramen.

Anecdotes from the Film Industry

A Study of the Costumes of a Hollywood Actress 208

— Huang Yingdai

The costumes of ordinary actresses in Hollywood are of course very beautiful. Among them, at least one actress spends £5,000 a year on her clothes.

This actress is Lilyan Tashman. She recently returned to Hollywood from Paris and New York, bringing eleven boxes of coats, underwear, and sportswear. But these clothes are not intended for use on the screen; they are just new clothes that she made before becoming Mrs. Edmund Lowe, before her wedding. Although she is very particular about clothing, she says to people:

(What I wear in my spare time is much simpler than what I wear on the screen. The workmanship and materials are not as exquisite as those on the screen.)

(When women all over the world see the clothes that I and other actresses wear on the screen, they rush to imitate them. This is completely wrong. The clothes on the screen are suitable for photography. If you wear these kinds of clothes on the street, they would inevitably be too flamboyant. They would be even more uncomfortable at home.)

She also told people that a woman's clothes must suit her figure. If she wears clothes that are excessively flamboyant, then all her actions must express a younger age, and she should walk faster. If her clothes are very dignified and trailing on the ground, then her body should be upright, making her look like a beautiful queen to others.

Film Magazine Revival

— Hong

The film craze of 1932 stirred up countless film publications. This was indeed an unprecedented initiative in China! Now, we have received such news again.

The film magazine published by Lianhua has been discontinued for a long time. This time, Luo Mingyou returned from Southeast Asia and, seeing the current state of the Chinese film industry, felt that Lianhua needed to re-establish its official magazine. Therefore, he specially invited Su Yi, a screenwriter from the First Studio, to be in charge of planning everything. Thus, Lianhua's film magazine will soon be announced to be revived.

The Story of William Powell 209

— Ai

William Powell was born in Pittsburgh. He collected and kept many rubber bands and old hats. He has his own swimming pool, fills it with cold water every day, and then jumps in. He has more clothes than any other male star in Hollywood, and loves to co-star with Kay Francis. Although he is madly in love with Carole Lombard, he usually objects to (prohibiting) the word. He thinks there should be a law to restrict the misuse of (prohibition).

Film Monograph

Methods for Actors to Train Themselves 211

— Chen Dabei

Here, I don't want to promote any kind of doctrine, nor do I plan to use a bunch of half-baked new terms to anesthetize the reader. I only feel that what the Chinese film industry urgently needs at present is new acting talent who can be original and not worship imitation.

Many people have already seen the importance of creating new talent, but who will create it? And what kind of creation method should be used? Hoping that the government will allocate public funds to establish a film school? No one dares to harbor such wishful thinking. If you expect film companies to take on this important task, that is also impossible. Because creating talent is not a profitable business. Therefore, even if a film company opens a training institute or training class or something similar, at most it will only save the film company from hiring extras. No film company would be willing to spend a lot of training fees to create talent for other film companies.

However, in the social news column of Shanghai newspapers, every year you can always find one or two cases of fraudulent financial gain under the guise of a film school. Each time, the number of students who are cheated is in the thousands or hundreds, you can know that, based on Shanghai alone, the number of people who hope to become movie stars is indeed not small. Counting the whole country, I don't know how many more there are. Among these many people, are there no talents to be made? It's a pity that they can't get proper research and practice methods. I am now using this space to introduce the various knowledge and methods of training oneself that movie actors must have, to these many enthusiasts who are unable to find a way in.
